\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0',\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1',\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2',\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4',\n  'five': '5',\n  'six': '6',\n  'seven': '7',\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9'\n};\n\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\n  if (!text) return '';\n digits += word;\n  }\n  // Also try raw digit extraction\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\n};\n\nexport const formatPhone = (d: string): string => {\n  const c = d.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3,6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\nconst const VoiceProvider: React.FC<{ children: ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n  const [lastHeard, setLastHeard] = useState('');\n  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  \n  const recognitionRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\n  const shouldListenRef = useRef(true);\n  const digitHandlerRef = useRef<((d: string) => void) | null>(null);\n  const commandHandlerRef = useRef<((c: string) => void) | null>(null);\n  \n  // Initialize speech recognition\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SR) {\n      setError('Speech recognition not supported');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    const recognition = new SR();\n    recognition.continuous = true;\n    recognition.interimResults = true;\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n    recognitionRef.current = recognition;\n    synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\n    \n    recognition.onstart = () => {\n      console.log('[MR.V] \ud83c\udfa4 LISTENING');\n      setIsListening(true);\n      setIsPaused(false);\n      setError(null);\n    };\n    \n    recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\n      \n      if (text) {\n        setTranscript(text);\n        console.log('[MR.V] Heard:', text, 'final:', result.isFinal);\n        \n        if (result.isFinal) {\n          setLastHeard(text);\n          const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n          \n          // Global commands\n          if (lower.includes('hey') || lower.includes('stop') || lower.includes('pause')) {\n            console.log('[MR.V] \u23f8\ufe0f PAUSE command');\n            shouldListenRef.current = false;\n            recognition.stop();\n            setIsPaused(true);\n            return;\n          }\n digits);\n            digitHandlerRef.current(digits);\n          }\n          \n          // Send command\n          if (commandHandlerRef.current) {\n            commandHandlerRef.current(lower);\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    };\n    \n    recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\n      console.log('[MR.V] Error:', event.error);\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n        setError('Microphone blocked. Click \ud83d\udd12 to allow.');\n        setIsListening(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    recognition.onend = () => {\n      console.log('[MR.V] Recognition ended, shouldListen:', shouldListenRef.current);\n      if (shouldListenRef.current && !isSpeaking) {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          if (shouldListenRef.current && recognitionRef.current) {\n            try { recognitionRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\n          }\n        }, 100);\n      } else {\n        setIsListening(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    // Auto-start after short delay\n    try { recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    };\n  }, []);\n  \n  // Speak function\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string, onComplete?: () => void) => {\n    if (!text || !synthRef.current) utterance.pitch = 1.0;\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\n    \n    // Try to get a good voice\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US'));\n    if && recognitionRef.current) {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          try { recognitionRef.current?.start(); } catch(e) {}\n        }, 300);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    utterance.onerror = () => {\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\n      onComplete?.();\n    };\n    \n    synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\n  }, [isListening]);\n  \n  const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => {\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\n    setIsSpeaking(false);\n  }, []);\n  \n  const startListening = useCallback(() => {\n    shouldListenRef.current = true;\n    setIsPaused(false);\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\n      try { recognitionRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n  }, []);\n  \n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\n    shouldListenRef.current = false;\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    setIsListening(false);\n  }, []);\n  \n  const pause = useCallback(() => {\n    shouldListenRef.current = false;\n    setIsPaused(true);\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n  }, []);\n  \n  const resume = useCallback(() => {\n    shouldListenRef.current = true;\n    setIsPaused(false);\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\n      try { recognitionRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n  }, []);\n  \n  const registerDigitHandler = useCallback((handler: (d: string) => void) => {\n    digitHandlerRef.current = handler;\n  }, []);\n  \n  const registerCommandHandler = useCallback((handler: (c: string) => void) => {\n    commandHandlerRef.current = handler;\n  }, []);\n  \n  const unregisterHandlers = useCallback(() => {\n    digitHandlerRef.current = null;\n    commandHandlerRef.current = null;\n  }, []);\n  \n  return (\n    <VoiceContext.Provider value={{\n      isListening, isSpeaking, isPaused, transcript, lastHeard, error,\n      speak, stopSpeaking, startListening, stopListening, pause, resume,\n      registerDigitHandler, registerCommandHandler, unregisterHandlers\n    }}>\n      {children}\n    </VoiceContext.Provider>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default VoiceContext;\nCTXEOF\n\necho \" Tell me your phone number again.');\n    }\n  }, [value, onChange, onNext, voice]);\n  \n  // Register handlers\n  useEffect(() => {\n    voice.registerDigitHandler(handleDigits);\n    voice.registerCommandHandler(handleCommand);\n    return () => voice.unregisterHandlers();\n  }, [handleDigits, handleCommand, voice]);\n  \n  // Welcome message\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!spokenRef.current) {\n      spokenRef.current = true;\n      setTimeout(() => {\n        voice.speak('Welcome! WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0',\\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1',\\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2',\\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4',\\n  'five': '5',\\n  'six': '6',\\n  'seven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9'\\n};\\n\\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\\n  if (!text) return '';\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\\\s+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  for (const word of words) {\\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\\n    else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(word)) digits += word;\\n  }\\n  // Also try raw digit extraction\\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\\n};\\n\\nexport const formatPhone = (d: string): string => {\\n  const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3,6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// Context\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nconst VoiceContext = createContext<VoiceContextType | null>(null);\\n\\nexport const useVoiceContext = () => {\\n  const ctx = useContext(VoiceContext);\\n  if (!ctx) throw new Error('useVoiceContext must be inside VoiceProvider');\\n  return ctx;\\n};\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// Provider\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nexport const VoiceProvider: React.FC<{ children: ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [lastHeard, setLastHeard] = useState('');\\n  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\\n  \\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n  const shouldListenRef = useRef(true);\\n  const digitHandlerRef = useRef<((d: string) => void) | null>(null);\\n  const commandHandlerRef = useRef<((c: string) => void) | null>(null);\\n  \\n  // Initialize speech recognition\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SR) {\\n      setError('Speech recognition not supported');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    const recognition = new SR();\\n    recognition.continuous = true;\\n    recognition.interimResults = true;\\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n    recognitionRef.current = recognition;\\n    synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\\n    \\n    recognition.onstart = () => {\\n      console.log('[MR.V] \\ud83c\\udfa4 LISTENING');\\n      setIsListening(true);\\n      setIsPaused(false);\\n      setError(null);\\n    };\\n    \\n    recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n      \\n      if (text) {\\n        setTranscript(text);\\n        console.log('[MR.V] Heard:', text, 'final:', result.isFinal);\\n        \\n        if (result.isFinal) {\\n          setLastHeard(text);\\n          const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n          \\n          // Global commands\\n          if (lower.includes('hey') || lower.includes('stop') || lower.includes('pause')) {\\n            console.log('[MR.V] \\u23f8\\ufe0f PAUSE command');\\n            shouldListenRef.current = false;\\n            recognition.stop();\\n            setIsPaused(true);\\n            return;\\n          }\\n          \\n          // Extract and send digits\\n          const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n          if (digits && digitHandlerRef.current) {\\n            console.log('[MR.V] \\ud83d\\udcf1 Digits:', digits);\\n            digitHandlerRef.current(digits);\\n          }\\n          \\n          // Send command\\n          if (commandHandlerRef.current) {\\n            commandHandlerRef.current(lower);\\n          }\\n        }\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      console.log('[MR.V] Error:', event.error);\\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n        setError('Microphone blocked. Click \\ud83d\\udd12 to allow.');\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    recognition.onend = () => {\\n      console.log('[MR.V] Recognition ended, shouldListen:', shouldListenRef.current);\\n      if (shouldListenRef.current && !isSpeaking) {\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          if (shouldListenRef.current && recognitionRef.current) {\\n            try { recognitionRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n          }\\n        }, 100);\\n      } else {\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    // Auto-start after short delay\\n    setTimeout(() => {\\n      if (shouldListenRef.current) {\\n        try { recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n      }\\n    }, 1000);\\n    \\n    return () => {\\n      shouldListenRef.current = false;\\n      try { recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    };\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  // Speak function\\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string, onComplete?: () => void) => {\\n    if (!text || !synthRef.current) return;\\n    \\n    console.log('[MR.V] \\ud83d\\udd0a Speaking:', text);\\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\\n    \\n    // Pause recognition while speaking\\n    if (recognitionRef.current && isListening) {\\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\\n    \\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\\n    utterance.pitch = 1.0;\\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\\n    \\n    // Try to get a good voice\\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US'));\\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\\n    \\n    utterance.onend = () => {\\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\\n      onComplete?.();\\n      // Resume listening after speaking\\n      if (shouldListenRef.current && recognitionRef.current) {\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          try { recognitionRef.current?.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n        }, 300);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    utterance.onerror = () => {\\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\\n      onComplete?.();\\n    };\\n    \\n    synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\\n  }, [isListening]);\\n  \\n  const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => {\\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n    setIsSpeaking(false);\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const startListening = useCallback(() => {\\n    shouldListenRef.current = true;\\n    setIsPaused(false);\\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n      try { recognitionRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\\n    shouldListenRef.current = false;\\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    setIsListening(false);\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const pause = useCallback(() => {\\n    shouldListenRef.current = false;\\n    setIsPaused(true);\\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const resume = useCallback(() => {\\n    shouldListenRef.current = true;\\n    setIsPaused(false);\\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n      try { recognitionRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const registerDigitHandler = useCallback((handler: (d: string) => void) => {\\n    digitHandlerRef.current = handler;\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const registerCommandHandler = useCallback((handler: (c: string) => void) => {\\n    commandHandlerRef.current = handler;\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const unregisterHandlers = useCallback(() => {\\n    digitHandlerRef.current = null;\\n    commandHandlerRef.current = null;\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  return (\\n    <VoiceContext.Provider value={{\\n      isListening, isSpeaking, isPaused, transcript, lastHeard, error,\\n      speak, stopSpeaking, startListening, stopListening, pause, resume,\\n      registerDigitHandler, registerCommandHandler, unregisterHandlers\\n    }}>\\n      {children}\\n    </VoiceContext.Provider>\\n  );\\n};\\n\\nexport default VoiceContext;\\nCTXEOF\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 VoiceContext.tsx created\\\"\\n\\n#
